<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h1 class="english">Bernalillo County Metropolitan Court</h1></div>

<div class="et_pb_main_blurb_image"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap"><span class="et-waypoint et_pb_animation_off et_pb_animation_off_tablet et_pb_animation_off_phone et-pb-icon">a</span></span></div>

<div class="et_pb_title_container">
<h1 class="entry-title">Home</h1>
</div>
</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_2 et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p style="font-weight: 400;text-align: center"><strong>**Effective Monday, July 25, 2022, Judge Linda S. Rogers will take over Judge David A. Murphys misdemeanor docket, and Division XVI (previously Judge Murphys) will become a Felony Division.**</strong></p>
<h3 style="text-align: center"><span style="color: #800000"><strong>Mask Requirements:</strong></span></h3>
<h4 style="text-align: center"><i>Masks are no longer required to enter the courthouse. However, masks must be worn while appearing in a courtroom or the jury assembly area.</i></h4>
<hr />
<h3 style="text-align: center"><span style="color: #800000"><strong>COVID Screening:</strong></span></h3>
<h4 style="text-align: center"><em>If you are app</em><em>earing in-person at the Metropolitan Court, please complete the required COVID-19 Screening Questions on THE DAY that you are scheduled to appear in court by </em><span style="color: #ff0000"><em><a href="https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSelodXIywC26ZMZiGvn1jI4nAoWbbD96xOvlmuy332vL22K1Q/viewform" target="_blank" rel="noopener">clicking here.</a><br /></em></span><span style="color: #ff0000"><strong><em></em></strong></span></h4>
<hr />
<h3 style="text-align: center"><span style="color: #800000"><strong>Virtual Court:</strong></span><span style="color: #ff0000"><strong><em></em></strong></span></h3>
<h4 style="text-align: center"><span style="color: #000000"><em>To access the Virtual Hearing Links, please <strong><a href="https://metro.nmcourts.gov/bernalillo-county-metropolitan-court/virtual-hearing-links/">click here.</a></strong></em></span></h4>
<hr /></div>

<h2 class="et_pb_slide_title"><a href="https://metro.nmcourts.gov/2022/07/11/judge-asra-i-elliott-sworn-in-as-metropolitan-court-judge/">Judge Asra I. Elliott sworn in as Metropolitan Court Judge</a></h2><div class="et_pb_slide_content"><p>Judge Asra I. Elliott was sworn in as a Bernalillo County Metropolitan Court Judge last week after her recent appointment by Governor Lujan Grisham. Judge Elliott was appointed to Division I of the court and will hear misdemeanor criminal cases and felony first appearances. She succeeds Judge Victor E. Valdez, who retired in May.</p></div>

<h4 class="et_pb_slide_title"><a href="https://metro.nmcourts.gov/bernalillo-county-metropolitan-court/news/the-metro-beat/monthly-legal-clinics-continue-virtually/">Monthly Legal Clinics Continue Virtually</a></h4><div class="et_pb_slide_content"><p>The Metropolitan Court continues to host FREE monthly legal clinics the second Friday of each month from 10:00 a.m. to 1:00 p.m. Volunteer attorneys are available telephonically to provide free civil legal advice in the following areas of law: Landlord/Tenant, Consumer Rights, Trial Preparation, Employee Wage Claims, Debt/Bankruptcy and/or Discovery.</p></div>
<div class="et_pb_button_wrapper"><a class="et_pb_button et_pb_more_button" href="https://metro.nmcourts.gov/bernalillo-county-metropolitan-court/news/the-metro-beat/monthly-legal-clinics-continue-virtually/">Click Here</a></div>

<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_3 et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2><span>COVID-19 Information &amp; Updates</span></h2></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_accordion et_pb_accordion_0">
<div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_0 et_pb_toggle_open">
<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title"> I have a traffic ticket:</h3>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>You have received a traffic citation.  Rather than coming to court on the date and time of your scheduled Traffic Arraignment, please call 1-346-248-7799 and use Webinar ID number: 925 4007 8987 and press #.  It will ask you for a participant ID, but press # instead to connect.  </p>
<p>When you call the number above on the date and time of your scheduled Traffic Arraignment, you will speak with a special prosecutor appointed by the Bernalillo County District Attorney who is available to discuss options in your case and negotiate a possible plea agreement with you. The special prosecutor is not a court employee and will only speak with you on the date and time set on your traffic citation(s).</p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_1 et_pb_toggle_close">
<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">I have a court hearing:</h3>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><span style="color: #000000">Some hearings are still being held remotely. Per <a href="https://metro.nmcourts.gov/wp-content/uploads/sites/39/2022/05/Order-No.-22-8500-018-and-Protocols-Amending-PHE-Protocol-Nos.-1-2-3_-eff.-3-24-22.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Supreme Court Order No. 22-8500-018</a>, appearances by phone are only allowed if the presiding judge has found &#8220;compelling circumstances&#8221; that the person is unable to appear by video. </span>To access the Virtual Hearing Links, please <strong><a href="https://metro.nmcourts.gov/bernalillo-county-metropolitan-court/virtual-hearing-links/">click here.</a></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: left">If you enconter any issues or have additional questions, please call our Customer Service Division at (505) 841-8151.  Updated case information can be found at:<span> </span><a href="https://caselookup.nmcourts.gov/caselookup/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">https://caselookup.nmcourts.gov/caselookup/</a>.</p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_2 et_pb_toggle_close">
<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">I&#039;m a juror:</h3>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><h2 style="text-align: center"><span style="color: #ff0000"><strong>ATTENTION JURORS:</strong></span></h2>
<p style="text-align: center"><span style="color: #ff0000"><strong>Jury trials have resumed, however, you will </strong></span><span style="color: #000000"><strong><u>NOT</u></strong><strong> </strong></span><span style="color: #ff0000"><strong>be reporting to the courthouse in-person on your first day of jury service.  Jurors are to call our Jury Message Phone Line at 505-841-8158 each day between the hours of 9:45 a.m. and 10:15 a.m. through the end of their term.  Please have the sequence number that is listed on your summons with you when you call. </strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align: center"><span style="color: #ff0000"><strong>In the event that a panel of jurors is selected and instructed to report to the courthouse, your report time will be no later than 11:00 a.m.</strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align: center"><span style="color: #000000">Your jury service is important, and we want to assure you that the court is continuing to adhere to COVID-19 Safe Practices.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center"><span style="color: #000000">If you have experienced  symptoms of COVID-19 such as; a fever, cough, shortness of breath, or have been diagnosed  with COVID-19 in the past 5 days, <strong>OR</strong> have been in contact with someone with the virus, or traveled outside of the United States within the past 7 days, please call the courts Jury Division at 505-841-8141.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center"><span style="color: #000000">A week before your jury term, you will receive an e-notification from the Jury Division providing you with current juror reporting information.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center"><span style="color: #000000"> If you need to provide the court with an email address/text number, or if you did not receive the courts communication in this timeframe or have any other questions, please call 505-841-8141.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center"><span style="color: #000000"> If instructed to report in-person, jurors may NOT bring into the Bernalillo County Metropolitan Courthouse: electronics (except as allowed below), cameras, glass containers, or weapons of any kind including, but not limited to, guns, knives, pepper spray, metal nail files, razor blades, or metal eating utensils. Jurors MAY bring cell phones, computers, and tablets; provided, however, that Jurors may NOT use those devices to take photos or record while in the Courthouse. Jurors are permitted to bring in food or drink as long as it is not a glass container.</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center"><span style="color: #000000">Thank you for your jury service.</span></p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_3 et_pb_toggle_close">
<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">I&#039;m a witness:</h3>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><span style="color: #000000">Some hearings are still being held remotely. Per <a href="https://metro.nmcourts.gov/wp-content/uploads/sites/39/2022/05/Order-No.-22-8500-018-and-Protocols-Amending-PHE-Protocol-Nos.-1-2-3_-eff.-3-24-22.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Supreme Court Order No. 22-8500-018</a>, appearances by phone are only allowed if the presiding judge has found &#8220;compelling circumstances&#8221; that the person is unable to appear by video. </span>To access the Virtual Hearing Links, please <strong><a href="https://metro.nmcourts.gov/bernalillo-county-metropolitan-court/virtual-hearing-links/">click here.</a></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: left">If you enconter any issues or have additional questions, please call our Customer Service Division at (505) 841-8151.  Updated case information can be found at:<span> </span><a href="https://caselookup.nmcourts.gov/caselookup/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">https://caselookup.nmcourts.gov/caselookup/</a>.</p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_4 et_pb_toggle_close">
<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">I&#039;m on Probation/ Pretrial Supervision:</h3>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>Please contact your probation officer as soon as possible to discuss options.</p>
<p>For general information, please call: (505) 841-8189.</p>
<p>For information regarding Felony Pretrial Supervision, please call: (505) 841-8248.</p>
<p>For contact information for the various requirements of the DWI First Offender Program at Metro Court, please click<span> </span><a href="/wp-content/uploads/sites/39/2020/12/FOP-Flier.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">here</a>. </p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_5 et_pb_toggle_close">
<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">Online Filing &amp; Faxing:</h3>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>Weve made it easier to conduct court business from home.</p>
<p>Metro Court is now accepting pleadings via email at: <span style="text-decoration: underline"><strong><a href="mailto:metrpleadings@nmcourts.gov" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">metrpleadings@nmcourts.gov</a></strong></span> or via fax at: (505) 222-4831.</p>
<p><strong>This email and fax are only to be used to send Motions or other pleadings to the Court. This is not to be used for a direct email to the Judge</strong>. Copies of your pleading/motion need to be attached to the email, and you also need to send a copy to the opposing party or officer/prosecutor on your case. If you have an attorney, you may want to discuss your motion or pleading with your attorney before you email/fax the Court.</p>
<p>Please remember when emailing your motion/pleading to the court to include your name and case number in the subject line. The Court will inform you in writing if your motion/request has been approved, or you may call Customer Service at (505) 841-8151 to check on the status of your motion/request.</p>
<p>In addition to the four (4) forms below, there are additional forms available on our <a href="https://metro.nmcourts.gov/bernalillo-county-metropolitan-court/self-help/self-help-center/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="text-decoration: underline"><strong>Self-Help Center page</strong></span>.</a></p>
<p>If you would like to use one of the Motions below, click on the links and either print the form or motion or fill it out online and follow the instructions below.</p>
<p style="text-align: left"><strong>&#8211;<a href="https://metro.nmcourts.gov/wp-content/uploads/sites/39/2022/02/CR-30-Motion-for-Continuance-2-7-22.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span style="text-decoration: underline">Motion for Continuance</span>;</a></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: left"><strong>&#8211;<a href="/wp-content/uploads/sites/39/2020/12/Motion-for-Extension-CR-130-3-30-20.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span style="text-decoration: underline">Motion for Extension</span>;</a></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: left"><strong>&#8211;<a href="/wp-content/uploads/sites/39/2020/12/Request-for-Audio-or-Audio-Visual-Appearance-CR-104-Revised-2-24-091.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span style="text-decoration: underline">Request for Telephonic Hearing</span></a>; </strong>and/or</p>
<p style="text-align: left"><strong>&#8211;<span style="text-decoration: underline"><a href="https://metro.nmcourts.gov/wp-content/uploads/sites/39/2021/08/CV179-Blank-Motion.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Blank Motion</a></span></strong></p>
<p>To complete the forms, you must have or install Adobe Acrobat on your computer or phone.   For help using Adobe Acrobat Reader to complete and email the forms from your phone, please see the instructional videos below for Android and iPhone devices:</p>
<p><a href="https://youtu.be/bDITwIQdaw4" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">https://youtu.be/bDITwIQdaw4</a> (iPhone)<br /><a href="https://youtu.be/Ot9KaiKM4J0" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">https://youtu.be/Ot9KaiKM4J0</a> (Android)</p>
<p>Visit your app store to download Adobe Acrobat:</p>
<p><a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.adobe.reader&amp;hl=en_US" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.adobe.reader&amp;hl=en_US</a><br /><a href="https://apps.apple.com/us/app/adobe-acrobat-reader-for-pdf/id469337564" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">https://apps.apple.com/us/app/adobe-acrobat-reader-for-pdf/id469337564</a></p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_6 et_pb_toggle_close">
<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">Online Schools &amp; Services:</h3>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>For information on court-ordered schools and services now available online, please call (505) 841-8151.</p>
<p>The full list is available <a href="https://metro.nmcourts.gov/wp-content/uploads/sites/39/2022/03/Metros-List-of-Online-Services-2-25-2022.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">here</a>.</p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_7 et_pb_toggle_close">
<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">I need to pay court fines and fees:</h3>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><span>Court fines and fees can be paid online at: </span><a href="https://publicaccess.nmcourts.gov/default.aspx" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">https://publicaccess.nmcourts.gov/default.aspx</a><span>.</span></p>
<p><span>You may also pay court fines and fees by mailing in a personal check, cashiers check or money order to:</span></p>
<p><span>The Bernalillo County Metropolitan Court</span><br /><span>401 Lomas Blvd. NW</span><br /><span>Albuquerque, NM 87102</span></p>
<p><span>*Checks should be made out to the Bernalillo County Metropolitan Court, and please note your case number on the check.</span></p>
<p><span>For questions, please call: (505) 841-8151.</span></p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_8 et_pb_toggle_close">
<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">Im requesting a court document:</h3>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><span>If you would like to request a court document, please visit our Public Records Request Page at: <a href="https://metro.nmcourts.gov/bernalillo-county-metropolitan-court/public-records-request/">https://metro.nmcourts.gov/bernalillo-county-metropolitan-court/public-records-request/</a></span></p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_9 et_pb_toggle_close">
<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">I need to serve a Notice of Appeal on the court monitor:</h3>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><span>With </span><span>the ongoing COVID-19 pandemic, the Court realizes that it may present</span><span> </span><span>a challenge for the parties</span><span> </span><span>to serve the Metropolitan Court&#8217;s court monitor in appeals of record cases to the Court of Appeals</span><span>. Therefore, the Metropolitan Court created an email group </span><span>(</span><a href="mailto:metrappeals-grp@nmcourts.gov" target="_blank" rel="noopener">metrappeals-grp@nmcourts.gov</a><span>) that </span><span>facilitates service of the Notice of Appeal only to the &#8220;court monitor or court reporter.&#8221; However, this email group does not replace the process of filing the Notice of Appeal or any other pleadings with the Metropolitan Court.  So please continue to file pleadings with a copy for the Judge as you would normally file pleadings. </span></p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_10 et_pb_toggle_close">
<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">Metropolitan Court COVID-19 Operations Plan (March 2022)</h3>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><a href="https://metro.nmcourts.gov/wp-content/uploads/sites/39/2022/03/Metropolitan-Court-COVID-19-Operations-Plan-Effective-3-21-2022-FINAL-Revised.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Metropolitan Court COVID-19 Operations Plan (March 2022)</a></p></div>
</div>
